<div id="review_257210091" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/257210091" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/257210091?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=tortured-souls">tortured-souls</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=big-misunderstanding">big-misunderstanding</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=fabulous-secondary-characters">fabulous-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=arrogant-cocky-hero">arrogant-cocky-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=4-star">4-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=frustrating-hero">frustrating-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer257210091" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17309429281825780178"><b> 3 1/2 Stars</b><br/><br/><i>Golden Trail</i> is another good book by Kristen Ashley, and though it was not my favorite, it still captured my imagination with vivid characters, a well developed plot, intriguing suspense, and passionate love scenes. That said, I felt something was missing from the story, and it took me some time to figure out what that was. For me, what was missing was the tantalizingly delicious romance between the hero and heroine, that I feel can be deliver only through the heroine the perspective</span>
  <span id="freeText17309429281825780178" style="display:none"><b> 3 1/2 Stars</b><br /><br /><i>Golden Trail</i> is another good book by Kristen Ashley, and though it was not my favorite, it still captured my imagination with vivid characters, a well developed plot, intriguing suspense, and passionate love scenes. That said, I felt something was missing from the story, and it took me some time to figure out what that was. For me, what was missing was the tantalizingly delicious romance between the hero and heroine, that I feel can be deliver only through the heroine the perspective. Let me explain.<br /><br />I love the passionate and all-consuming romances inherent in all Kristen Ashley books, and for me, that romance is enhanced through the heroines point of view. As a woman, I'm able to identify and related with the heroine in a way that I'm not able to with the hero. By having some time in the heroine's head, so to speak, I'm allowed to see the hero through the heroine's eyes and experience on an emotional level all the thoughts, feelings, and sensations the heroine has for the hero. <br /><br />Don't get me wrong, I loved being in Layne's head; after all, Kristen Ashley writes heroes like no one else. But, Layne simply could not deliver the sexy, swoonalicious hero that Rocky's voice could have achieved. <br /><br />I did have one major issue with Layne—his fathering skills. I was not impressed with him as a father. He left his two young boys to be raised by his ex-wife for 12 years, finally returning home to become more active in their lives. Layne then involves the boys, ages 14 and 17, in a dangerous undercover operation. So NOT cool, Layne! <br /><br />The best part of the story for me was the last few chapters of the book and the epilogue. They were simply fantastic. The epilogue left me with a huge smile on my face and the genuine hope for a invitation to Jasper and Keira's wedding in one of Kristen Ashley's upcoming book. *Hint, Hint*<br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17309429281825780178" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2687131024?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" href="/user/show/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth">Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2687131024" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15630661722050175172">3.5 STARS<br/><br/>I loved Layne, I liked Rocky, I also enjoyed the male POV but would have liked some insight into Rocky's mind - the reason why she left Layne came to light only late in the book and the way it did...I wasn't a fan of that. I also wasn't a fan of Rocky's dad and brother, not telling Layne the reason why Rocky left and serving up attitude when Layne had to deal with the consequences.<br/><br/>I loved Layne with his sons but involving them into dangerous cases he worked? Uh. <br/><br/>I still liked the story </span>
  <span id="freeText15630661722050175172" style="display:none">3.5 STARS<br /><br />I loved Layne, I liked Rocky, I also enjoyed the male POV but would have liked some insight into Rocky's mind - the reason why she left Layne came to light only late in the book and the way it did...I wasn't a fan of that. I also wasn't a fan of Rocky's dad and brother, not telling Layne the reason why Rocky left and serving up attitude when Layne had to deal with the consequences.<br /><br />I loved Layne with his sons but involving them into dangerous cases he worked? Uh. <br /><br />I still liked the story line a lot and there were some beautifully emotional scenes that are typical for KA.</span>

<div id="review_334684503" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/334684503" />
    <a title="Karen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6972914-karen"><img alt="Karen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529600203p2/6972914.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/334684503?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karen" href="/user/show/6972914-karen">Karen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer334684503" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11554957671160545640"><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/MarcoDapper009_zps8d45bc30.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909868i/3183622.jpg' alt='Marco Dapper photo MarcoDapper009_zps8d45bc30.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>He felt something sweep through him, an emotion that he didn't quite get, but one he liked, and it rushed through him strong, leaving a golden trail..</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>**sigh**.....so flippin' sweet!!!! Absolutely LOVED IT!!! 5 Golden Shining Stars</b><br/> <br/>This was yet another example of the genius that is Kristen Ashley. And the title literally says it all, because it not only left Golden Trails blazing through Tanner Layne's soul, but in mine as well. There were so many incredible moments and swoon</span>
  <span id="freeText11554957671160545640" style="display:none"><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/MarcoDapper009_zps8d45bc30.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909868i/3183622.jpg" alt="Marco Dapper photo MarcoDapper009_zps8d45bc30.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>He felt something sweep through him, an emotion that he didn't quite get, but one he liked, and it rushed through him strong, leaving a golden trail..</i>
</b><br><br><b>**sigh**.....so flippin' sweet!!!! Absolutely LOVED IT!!! 5 Golden Shining Stars</b><br> <br>This was yet another example of the genius that is Kristen Ashley. And the title literally says it all, because it not only left Golden Trails blazing through Tanner Layne's soul, but in mine as well. There were so many incredible moments and swoon worthy scenes that I was completely lost in the story. I actually felt like I was 'living' this story with the characters. And what a treat it was reading the story from Layne's point of view. He was such an incredible guy. I think I fell in love with him right along with our heroine!<br><br>Tanner Layne is a divorced 42 year old ex-cop turned PI, living in the 'Burg with his two teenage son's Jasper and Tripp. The story opens with him waking up in the hospital after being shot 3 times during an investigation of a suspected dirty cop in the force. He wakes after having an erotic dream of his first love, Raquel "Rocky" Merrick, who he hasn't been with for 18 years, but has never really gotten over. When he wakes after this dream, he finds her sitting in his hospital room. <br><br>Rocky, now 38, is married to someone else, and has been for the last 10 years. So why is she there? Layne is confused, not only by this dream of her he just had, but also by her presence in his room. He is still bitter about the way they left things 18 years ago, and hasn't even spoken to her in some time. And so the story begins...<br><br><b>
  <i>Had eighteen years to learn to how to be the one who does the fucking, not the one who gets fucked."</i>
</b><br><br>Yep, he's bitter. She broke his heart 18 years ago and gave him NO explanation for it. And it seems she wants back in? What about her husband, Dr. Jarrod Astley? He doesn't trust her, and he still wants answers... answers that he just can't seem to get. But he can't seem to hold back his feelings for her.. Rocky, now filing for divorce herself, makes it clear she wants back in his life, and he sees an opportunity at happiness, but can he trust it?<br><br><b>
  <i>This time, baby with my boys in the mix, you can't cut us loose and go your merry fuckin' way because I'm not gonna let you cut us loose."</i>
</b><br><br>And those boys!!! Jasper "Jas" and Tripp... OMG they were just pure fucking GOLD!!! I love those boys!!!!! Jas is 17, and is so cocky and cool like his dad, and Tripp, who is 14 is also very good looking but much more sweet and innocent... learnin' cool, but not quite there yet! These two completely captured my heart in the story. If only teenagers could really be this good!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>Jasper- "You cool with Kierry bein' here when you're not?" "Just as long as I don't have to set up a crib in the corner of your bedroom, that is, if I win at hand to hand combat defendin' my son against a gonzo Joe Callahan," Layne answered. Jasper grinned and crossed his cell phone over his heart before he lifted it in the air, "Swear. Gentleman. Totally."<br>Layne stared at his son then looked to Tripp who was also grinning at him and who decided to add, "Giselle Speakmon's parents are totally devout. When I get in there and we hook up, there won't be any cribs for me either, Dad, because I reckon they'll make her wear one of those chastity belts, knowin' Jas is my brother and all.</i>
</b><br><br>Then there is Dev.. Devin Glover, Layne's best friend and mentor, and older man in his early 60's, with a fabulously dry, cantankerous personality, who practically moved in. He had me laughing NON STOP!! Such a great character!!!! His first time meeting Layne's Mom was hilarious!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"She escape from an asylum?".... Well Vera huffed. "Who are you?"... "Devin Glover, friend of your boy's, retired PI and good judge of character."</i>
</b><br><br>Then there was the action...this story had so many bad things going on in the 'Burg it was difficult to keep up with them all. Even Layne seemed to have trouble keeping them all straight in his head. At first I though that this was going to bother me.. but as the story played out, it all just worked!!! <br><br>And I can't leave this review without mentioning Ryker... Another fabulous badass character that won my heart. <br><br><b>
  <i>Ryker to Layne..."Fuck me, bro, a badass who drinks sissy coffee and owns a yellow lab." His eyes came back to Layne, his attitude shut down and he grinned his ugly grin. "Gotta say, impressed you could pull that off."</i>
</b><br><br>So many incredible moments!!! I could go on for days. The story completely stole my heart, and I loved it all. The heartfelt moments and the subtle banter between the characters, and the total and complete goodness that is Tanner Layne!! <br><br><b>
  <i>Devin shook his head.<br>"What old man?"<br>"Just thinkin', thinkin' about a man who'd walk out a door and never turn back. Thinkin' about where he went, what he did and how it could never be worth losin' what he left behind. Your father is a grade A, one hundred percent, jackass, boy, turnin' his back and never knowin' the man you would become."</i>
</b><br><br>And then, THAT EPILOGUE!!!! It's RAININ' MEN!!!! Yep, only the Burg's finest.. wish I could have been at that BBQ!!<br><br><b>No less that 5 stars!!!! Complete Kristen Ashley GOLD!!!!</b><br><br><b>Tanner Layne</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/MarcoDapper002_zps51d9d046.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909868i/3183624._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo MarcoDapper002_zps51d9d046.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Raquel Merrick</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/EmilyDidonato11_zps30cb2e2f.jpeg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909868i/3183625._SY540_.jpg" alt="Emily Didonato photo EmilyDidonato11_zps30cb2e2f.jpeg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11554957671160545640" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_299851938" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/299851938" />
    <a title="Mimi Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith"><img alt="Mimi Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1297016674p2/4884889.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/299851938?book_show_action=true">Mar 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mimi Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mimi Smith" href="/user/show/4884889-mimi-smith">Mimi Smith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4884889-mimi-smith?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer299851938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12479542024086960268"><b>2.5 stars<br/><br/><i>Note-up to the last 10 percent this book was a 2 star read for me</i></b><br/><br/>I can't believe a KA book was so difficult for me to read. The problem was a combination of the drag effect, the annoying qualities of the characters and, well, other things. So, for once, a serious review of a KA book.<br/><br/>So my problems with...<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Layne</u>
</b><br/><br/>Oh, Layne, you never did redeem yourself. The entire book was written in the first person, his POV, so it was even more pronounced. So my problems:<br/><br/>1) Involving your girlfriend,</span>
  <span id="freeText12479542024086960268" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars<br /><br /><i>Note-up to the last 10 percent this book was a 2 star read for me</i></b><br /><br />I can't believe a KA book was so difficult for me to read. The problem was a combination of the drag effect, the annoying qualities of the characters and, well, other things. So, for once, a serious review of a KA book.<br /><br />So my problems with...<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Layne</u>
</b><br /><br />Oh, Layne, you never did redeem yourself. The entire book was written in the first person, his POV, so it was even more pronounced. So my problems:<br /><br />1) Involving your girlfriend, who's a teacher, in a mission<br />2)Involving your sons, ages 14 and 17, in an undercover investigation of a sex/prostitution of minors ring. What kind of a dad does that? You say they're almost adults, but geez!<br />3)Treating your mother in a not-so-nice fashion. I get taking a stand and defending your girlfriend, but it's your LOVING mother...<br />4)When your ex wife confronts you about the involvement of her sons in a case, you treat her like she's unreasonable, you know best, and you're the best dad in the world. She made mistakes, but you weren't around almost their whole lives! But of course, since this is a KA book, the ex is just jealous and a bitch(their words) who wants you for herself, not just a good mother. Of course. What else?<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Rocky</u>
</b><br /><br />Rocky left Layne 20 years ago, and almost the whole book, all we get is:<br /><br /><i>“Somethin’ means the world to you, you think one day you’ll lose it, you got two choices. You cut yourself off from it so, when you lose it, that don’t destroy you or you hold it so close, it can’t ever go away but, if it does, you got as many precious memories as you can bag. Thinkin’ about your girl, do either of those sound familiar?” <br /><br />“Why’d you leave me?” Her eyes held his, Layne held his breath and she surprised the fuck out of him when she answered. “I did it,” she stopped and licked her lips, “and I don’t know why I did it.”<br /><br />“She’s got somethin’ in her, Ma. Somethin’ not right and I gotta help her get it out but I don’t know what the fuck it is. I don’t even think Roc knows what it is. It made her leave me eighteen years ago and I know in my bones it’s gonna happen again, unless I sort that shit out, and all three of us are gonna lose her.</i><br /><br />And then we get, the explanation, she's ashamed of her periods and that's a root of a deeper issue. We learn the issue, but the whole thing wasn't explained the best IMO. What set it off before? How connected was it to the situation? After all the talk about us not knowing everything, and her pain and a deeper reason I expected a better explanation.<br /><br />Plus she's:<br /><br />1)Saint Rocky. Perfect teacher, organizes charity, is just a victim in life. Maybe the lack of her POV made all this more annoying?<br />2)She struts. A lot. Every time she moves she's strutting. I don't know who struts that much or why that's attractive, but couldn't she walk once in a while?<br />3)Her constant involvement in the investigation. TSTL, anyone? She goes off to attack and break in and who knows what else. Layne does call her on it...<br /><br /><i>“So, help me out in a way that actually helps me out. Be there for me and be smart. Those are the only two things you gotta do, easy enough for you but they’d mean a lot to me.”</i><br /><br />But at that point I was...whatever.<br /><br /><b>General, silly issue...</b><br /><br />Does everyone have to drop their g's and talk like that? No matter where they're from and are they educated or not they talk the same.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>I did like</u>
</b><br /><br />1) The kids. All of them.<br />2) Ryker. Now that's a swoon worthy hero.:D<br />3)The epilogue, of course.<br />4)The mystery was okay. <br /><br />All in all-disappointing for me for a KA book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12479542024086960268" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/716067016" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/716067016?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer716067016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4396490850334277170"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“If you are nothing else in this life, be wise, be compassionate, and be strong because those three are everything” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436146i/881461._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"You remembered."<br/><br/>His fingers curled around her neck and he put his forehead to hers before sharing, "I remembered, Rocky. I remember everything. I remember every...</i>fucking<i>...thing." <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4396490850334277170" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4 STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“If you are nothing else in this life, be wise, be compassionate, and be strong because those three are everything” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436146i/881461._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b><i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"You remembered."<br><br>His fingers curled around her neck and he put his forehead to hers before sharing, "I remembered, Rocky. I remember everything. I remember every...</i>fucking<i>...thing." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i></b>
</blockquote><br>This book was awesome! I very much enjoyed it. <b>Tanner Layne</b> and <b>Raquel 'Rocky' Merrick</b> were a young couple in love. Everyone knew they were meant to be. But one day, Rocky just leaves him without a word. It left him with a pain so big, that he never really got over it. But time went on, and eventually he did too. He is now a divorced father of two sons. The book starts with Layne waking up in a hospital after being shot and finding Rocky in the room with him. He wants her to leave and he doesn't want her to go. Rocky seems to want to get back together. Layne wants that too but doesn't want to get hurt. In his next case where he investigates a dirty cop, Rocky wants to be a part of that too. so they form a plan to pretend to be a couple in order to do so. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Live this with me, just live it, whatever happens, however it happens, just live it with me..." <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved Layne! He was a great man and trying his best at being a great father to his teenage boys. I absolutely LOVED that this whole book was in his POV. He was a total badass alpha and very dedicated to his work, but I loved that he also took the time to spend it with his sons, who were badasses in the making. I felt for him and the pain he went through after Rocky left him. Yes, he did move on with the mother of his sons and other women, but he never loved any other woman like he did Rocky. I loved the pace in which their relationship developed. It was slow but steady. And when the bow chika wow wow times started happening, it was so freaking hot and yet so sweet. I loved it and him!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433891ra/873482.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“Don’t let me leave you,” she whispered so quietly he almost didn’t hear her. <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Rocky was also such a great female character. She was strong yet broken from an event in her past. Which was quite a terrible event, my heart really broke for her, I can't even imagine going through that. And I couldn't believe that her family did nothing to help her get past that all these years. Despite all that, she was caring and loving towards others but I loved it when she was like that towards Layne's boys. I loved seeing them interact. She was in a loveless marriage and seeking for divorce, but her husband was not making it easy for her to get it. Never has she forgotten what she left behind with Layne, and now she wants to get it back, if he allows it. I really liked that when she let herself love, she made that person feel it. She was also quite protective and very capable in defending herself. I really liked her, and with Layne, they were perfect.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Okay, well...yesterday sucked and I didn't like watchin' you go through that, Rocky, and I was thinkin' last night about it and thinkin' I didn't like watchin' that but why wasn't because it sucked, you havin' to go through that but because you were hurting and I didn't like watchin' you hurt so I reckon that means I love you," Tripp announced...<br>"So see, stupid."<br><br>"Not stupid, baby, and thank you. That feeling is mutual... for both you guys."<br><br>"Cool," Tripp whispered.<br><br>"Yeah, cool," Jasper repeated also on a whisper.<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>There were quite a bit of subplots with all the investigative work Layne was doing. But also on the relationships of his two sons. I LOVED anything to do with Jas and Tripp, his boys were so AWESOME! I feel totally weird saying this about a teenage character, but I fell in love with Jas. He is gonna grow up to be one badass man, I just hope he gets a book when he is older, then I won't feel so weird about having a crush on him. I also loved Tripp, he was very endearing as the youngest brother and so sweet. I was happy that these two got a bit of a HEA of their own. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401264ra/778581.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Thank you, baby" she whispered.<br>"For what?" he whispered back.<br>"A beautiful life."<br><br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>What I didn't really like about this book, were the subplots on Layne's work. Not because it wasn't interesting, because it was, but because it became too much at times. I had a bit of a hard time following it all. I was like 'who's that guy again?' because there were so many characters involved. But otherwise, it was a very interesting storyline. I loved this book and loved it even more when Joe would appear *sigh*. I loved Layne and Rocky, especially when they would cuddle in bed. I loved his sons and the part they played in the story. The epilogue was so wonderful! I was very happy with it and I'm keeping my fingers crossed on Jas having his book. LOL! It was a really great read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4396490850334277170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1886883044" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13618011033814730092"><b>The book wasn't <i>bad</i></b> per se, but it wasn't <i>good</i> either. Though, surprisingly for the first time in a <b>KA</b> book I didn't feel like the book was <i>dragging</i>. Sure, it had its moments of boredom and was long, but it was alright. And it was kinda interesting to read a <b>KA</b> from the male's POV. <b>Raquel “Rocky” Merrick</b> (38)<br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Live this with me, just live it, whatever happens, however it happens, live it with me for two days. It doesn’t go the way you like, we’ll talk Monday night. It goes the way you lik</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText13618011033814730092" style="display:none"><b>The book wasn't <i>bad</i></b> per se, but it wasn't <i>good</i> either. Though, surprisingly for the first time in a <b>KA</b> book I didn't feel like the book was <i>dragging</i>. Sure, it had its moments of boredom and was long, but it was alright. And it was kinda interesting to read a <b>KA</b> from the male's POV. <b>Raquel “Rocky” Merrick</b> (38)<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Live this with me, just live it, whatever happens, however it happens, live it with me for two days. It doesn’t go the way you like, we’ll talk Monday night. It goes the way you like, we live it real and ride it out. Will you give me that, honey?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Tanner Layne</b> (42) was alright characters. Rocky was plain, cute, nice, wise and really kind. Layne was hot, knew what he wanted - went for it, honest, a great dad and had a soft spot. Btw, was I the only one who, when reading the blurb, first thought that Rocky was the male and Layne was the female? Layne isn't exactly a strong, powerful male name (even though it's his last name)... <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Men like you aren’t made, though, Tanner. Men like you just are.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I must say though, that I was <b>hugely disappointed</b> in the big <i>'secret'</i> that was hanging over Rocky and Layne's relationship and past. I had expected something more, something huge, but in the end, though it was bad and sad, it still wasn't all that... Overall, <b>it was alright</b>, but not something I'll re-read again and definitely not a favorite. I adored Layne's sons though!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If you are nothing else in this life, be wise, be compassionate, and be strong because those three are everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1487704980i/22043047.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Contemporary Romance<br><b>Series</b>: - Series (Standalone), Book Three<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Tanner Layne<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No.<br><b>Rating</b> - 2.5/3 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1638306941" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1638306941" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1638306941?book_show_action=true">May 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1638306941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16918906948658467874"><b>*** 3.44 ***<br/><br/>A buddy read with the KA addicts at BB&B</b><br/><br/>I love KA's ability to come up with and tell a story, as well as the talent to write some absolutely memorable characters... I love the magic she infuses in everything she writers... But this series has been dancing on my nerves!!! <br/><br/>In this book I didn't mind Lane being a possessive and pushy alpha jerk-off, nor that Rocky could be a total bitch with everyone but her man and the kids at school... I didn't love that, but it was OK. I didn't mind </span>
  <span id="freeText16918906948658467874" style="display:none"><b>*** 3.44 ***<br /><br />A buddy read with the KA addicts at BB&amp;B</b><br /><br />I love KA's ability to come up with and tell a story, as well as the talent to write some absolutely memorable characters... I love the magic she infuses in everything she writers... But this series has been dancing on my nerves!!! <br /><br />In this book I didn't mind Lane being a possessive and pushy alpha jerk-off, nor that Rocky could be a total bitch with everyone but her man and the kids at school... I didn't love that, but it was OK. I didn't mind the watered down reason for the first separation of the love birds, despite it being quite underwhelming and honestly, not very convincing... I didn't mind the fact that we are supposed to completely forgive and forget the fact that he was a terrible father for the majority of his children's lives and we have to accept that at ones he has transformed into the father of the century, while we have to accept that the woman who had and raised them into the good kids they are now is a total bitch and an inadequate parent.... I even don't mind that Kira is now dating Jazz and for her he transforms himself into a literal virgin, when previously he had fucked his way through the surrounding highschools in the area... <br /><br />What I had a difficult time accepting was the condescending way he would talk to his woman, but we were being told that that should be cute, the way he would wave every difference in opinion as silly, any strong opposition as adorable, but alas, so very wrong, since it is not what he thinks is best...<br />His blowing up on her brother and father were so over the top, it drove me to rage!!! Rocky was not the only one affected and grieving, they were all devastated... He was out of line and lost me at that moment...<br />Also, the constant put down of the mother of his children was just too much!!!! OK, we get the new chick is the one and only for you, but stop vilifying the woman who raised those perfect boys of yours all on her own, with no help from you, and now that you are around she is shit and you are perfect???? Bullshit!!! And making her into a villain was not enough, she has to be constantly reminded that she is fat now???<b> KA, love, what happened to not body-shaming women???</b> This really pissed me off. . ... <br /><br />As in the other books in this series, this book was too long for the plot it contains. But as all KA books, there is something that is in her writing that doesn't even allow for skimming... I have never been able to walk away from any of her books, although I got close the previous book in this series... She still wields her magic and I am still a fan... <br /><br />As a person who loves to recommend books, I take the same stand as my friend Robin , who is smart and wise beyond her years, and that is that I can not recommend her work, and this series in particular, because they are sooooo very love them or hate them, almost never in between. ... This series is just not as good as her others... So, if you have been thinking about starting to read KA , start with something else and read this when you run out of other of her works... <br /><br />I wish all Happy Reading and continue on with the hope for more uplifting books!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16918906948658467874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3135269770319193248">While I hate long seperations between couples, Rocky, Layne, and the kids really made up for it. I adored this family. Even though things weren't exactly as they seem in the beginning, to see a couple working together is what I love to read. Add in two teenage mini alpha's, Layne's sons, and you've got a winner.<br/><br/>Drama outside of the relationship is much preferable to me as a reader.   <span id="freeText3135269770319193248" style="display:none">While I hate long seperations between couples, Rocky, Layne, and the kids really made up for it. I adored this family. Even though things weren't exactly as they seem in the beginning, to see a couple working together is what I love to read. Add in two teenage mini alpha's, Layne's sons, and you've got a winner.<br /><br />Drama outside of the relationship is much preferable to me as a reader. Not that they didn't have drama in the relationship because they still had to work through what happened 18 years prior. However, I still felt like they were in it together and that's what made the difference.<br /><br />This one had a lot of great side characters that also added to my overall enjoyment of the book. There were a few minor things that I didn't like, but all the good outweighed the little irritations. <br /><br />I listened to the audiobook and highly recommend it. This author has a knack for picking out great narrators.</span>

<div id="review_561073139" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561073139" />
    <a title="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer"><img alt="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363047769p2/10459827.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561073139?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*" href="/user/show/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer">Jamie *Gypsy Smut-a-teer*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=protection-needed">protection-needed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10459827-jamie-gypsy-smut-a-teer?shelf=hot-in-here">hot-in-here</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561073139" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3459891614716344752">OMG,... Oh. My. GAWWWDDDD. I freakin' loved this book. Like LOVED IT!!!! I wish I could give it more stars.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Somethin' means the world to you, you think one day you'll lose it, you got tow choices. You cut yourself off from it so, when you lose it, that don't destroy you or hold it so close, it can't ever go away but, if it does, you got as many precious memories as you can bag. Thinkin' about your girl, do either of those sound familiar?"</i>
</b><br/><br/>Tanner Layne<br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413383i/813893._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"How many time do I have to tell you, </i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText3459891614716344752" style="display:none">OMG,... Oh. My. GAWWWDDDD. I freakin' loved this book. Like LOVED IT!!!! I wish I could give it more stars.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Somethin' means the world to you, you think one day you'll lose it, you got tow choices. You cut yourself off from it so, when you lose it, that don't destroy you or hold it so close, it can't ever go away but, if it does, you got as many precious memories as you can bag. Thinkin' about your girl, do either of those sound familiar?"</i>
</b><br><br>Tanner Layne<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413383i/813893._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"How many time do I have to tell you, sweetcheeks? I remember everything."</i>
</b><br><br>So, I'm kinda sorta at a loss for words here. I loved this book so much that I just can't put it into words. Kristen Ashley is genius once again, that I do know. <br><br>This story starts out with Layne and Rocky having an awkward conversation after years of separation. They had been madly in love 18 years prior, but for reasons Layne doesn't know she left, without a word. Despite his efforts, he lost her and in turn and not completely on purpose, started a different life without her. Now, laying in a hospital bed with three bullet wholes, he is wondering why she has showed up of a sudden. <br><br>Rocky<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413383i/813894._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"I was a child, and she was a child, in this kingdom by the sea; but we loved with a love that was more than a love~I and my Annabelle Lee."</b>
</i><br><br>Rocky also moved on. She's married to a wealthy doctor, teaches high school English lit, and lives in the rich part of town. Layne doesn't understand why all of a sudden she starts coming around but when invited over for a dinner and having a discussion with Rocky's brother, Layne decides he has to protect Rocky, mostly from herself, but also the trouble she has decided to put herself into. Layne and Rocky come to a deal, they pretend to be together in order to catch a dirty cop. Layne has already been on this case, but Rocky has become determined because her mother was murdered when she was fourteen, her brother and father are cops and she wants to take him down. But the longer Layne and Rocky pretend to be together, the more Layne is determined it goes from pretending to being real. <br><br>Jasper<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413383i/813895._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"It's good she hooked up with me, she's such a nut, she needs a badass to take her back."</i>
</b><br><br>So, I loved everything about this book. Ohmigod, the characters. Layne for sure and I loved getting the whole book in his POV. His kids, Jasper and Tripp are like my favorite New book kids, LOL!!! The more Layne and his boys grew closer and closer, the more they kicked ass. And then Rocky, I really wanted to hold a grudge against her. It drove me crazy not knowing for so long why she had up and left Layne. And a few times she threw a hissy and I was like, wait you did leave him, he has the right to have up a guard, but in the end I came around and ended up letting my grudge go. And then, getting to see more into Cal and Vi, and Colt and Feb. I really just could go on and on and on, but I really won't say a whole lot more except over and over how much I loved everything about this book. Btw, this series always makes me want to go to one of their back yard BBQ's and pop the top off my Budlight and get in on all the gossip. <br><br>Tripp &amp; Blondie<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413383i/813896._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Giselle Speakmon’s parents are totally devout. When I get in there and we hook up, there won’t be any cribs for me either, Dad, because I reckon they’ll make me wear one of those chastity belts, knowin’ Jas is my brother and all.”</i>
</b> <br><br>I don't want to spoil ANYTHING, about this book, because I don't want to ruin the read for anyone else, but definitely go read this. There was romance, friendship, suspense that tied into a storyline that drew me in and kept me guessing at every turn, hot sexy times, awesome characters, but mostly just plain ole simple KA awesomeness!!! I can't wait for more. :)<br><br><b>
  <i>“Any battle worth winnin’ is worth using every weapon available.”</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_271401551" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/271401551" />
    <a title="Searock" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6641663-searock"><img alt="Searock" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396402019p2/6641663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271401551?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Searock" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Searock" href="/user/show/6641663-searock">Searock</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=fabulous-in-every-way">fabulous-in-every-way</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=my-world-revolves-around-the-ka-sun">my-world-revolves-around-the-ka-sun</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271401551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8492579284278796922">Wow.<br/>Seems to me, when I use fewer words you guys appreciate it, so here goes my attempt at brevity (wish me luck cuz I freakin' loved this book).<br/><br/>A wonderful, satiating, KA experience (that's a brand now) with characters I love and a storyline that was complex but not complicated. All the good KA was here including interesting, quirky or familiar side characters and tons of active dialogue. I was laughing, grinning and enjoying every single page! <br/><br/>KA packed a lot of emotional stuff into this one w</span>
  <span id="freeText8492579284278796922" style="display:none">Wow.<br />Seems to me, when I use fewer words you guys appreciate it, so here goes my attempt at brevity (wish me luck cuz I freakin' loved this book).<br /><br />A wonderful, satiating, KA experience (that's a brand now) with characters I love and a storyline that was complex but not complicated. All the good KA was here including interesting, quirky or familiar side characters and tons of active dialogue. I was laughing, grinning and enjoying every single page! <br /><br />KA packed a lot of emotional stuff into this one without using much manipulation. It's usually the setup that seems hard to believe in the Burg books rather than the manipulation in the narrative and it holds true in Golden Trail as well. In this story, the things that take place prior to our meeting these characters is the part that feels more contrived. The unfolding plot and development of the characters actually felt totally authentic to me. <br /><br />The bottom line is KA is a story writing mamma jamma. <br /><br />The arc of this couple having been separated for years and now due to circumstances begin to deal with each other about that, is like the experience of watching a cold and hungry person step into a fire-warmed cabin and tuck into a big bowl of delicious love. <br /><br />The emergence from ruins is a great place to start a story and the Burg books all start there. I was shimmering with excitement to see the bleak condition of Layne's house when the story started... all rubbing my hands together with anticipation, I was.<br /><br />The characters are written with such a deft hand that every single one of them gets under your skin. The best part for me is that KA sure knows how to write men! They are absolutely to die for in this story. The mix of brawn, brain, guts, principles, possessiveness and devotion are over the top, but by no means overplayed or overwritten. They are just delightful and fun to read. <br /><br />Layne (H) seems like a terrible father and rather bleak as a human being, but we discovered he is deeply wounded by a lost love and has been in survival mode for 18 years. Also, the way he fathers his boys feels wrong at times, but through the narrative, I came to believe, for them, it was beyond right. This is what KA does that no one else can, this seemingly wrong behavior being right in a unique or special way... and I admit, I have gotten to the point of craving it (sounds kinda depraved, but its true).<br /><br />Rocky (h) was the best heroine. I could write paragraphs about her. She is bright and tough and yet she is quite vulnerable and needs Layne badly as he is the only one who has the stuff to help her through her unique battle.<br /><br />The only issues I ever seem to have with KA books are the background plots that at times interfere with my blissful suspension of disbelief. This time it was the storyline about a black market for underage sex-shenanigans that was tough to buy into, but that's okay. The KA experience is characters, characters, characters and the dynamics that occur between them via lots of scenes and very active dialogue. <br /><br />And the sexytimes in this one were off the chain. They're not drawn out or elaborate but they were frequent and they packed a punch.<br /><br />I'm a little shy to try and explain one amazing scene that revealed to me just how good this author is, but feel that I must: As reader, I was totally prepped for an eventual fallout that would stem from a trauma suffered by the h when she was very young. It's foreshadowed over and over and it was just a matter of time before the wheels fell off, so to speak. So anyway, I was reading along at a pretty good clip and then suddenly I saw it begin to rear its head in some innocuous scene. I could feel it in the tone and between the lines. It felt like a snake slithering around in the text. It was subtle and organic and beast was heading right toward these characters. But the H was onto it and did a masterful job of deflecting and sparring with this thing as though he was in a fight sequence but rather than physical, its purely visceral. Gee whiz, it was good writing. So good, I got the wow face. It wasn't the end of that issue, it didn't get tied up quite that neatly, but that first scene of it and the dialogue were riveting.<br /><br />Anyway, that's my attempt at brevity *snort*.<br />Oh, for those of you who don't like a lot of interruption in the dialogue that seems to plague KA novels, it's almost non-existent here (Ik, r?) Also the "mutter" exhaustion I suffered in the last book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_" title="At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a> (had over 100 occurrences of the word mutter- my kindle actually stopped counting beyond that) was not an issue in this one. Hey wait, that would make for a whopping drinking game! Prepare to be drunk for 3 days though...</span>
  <a data-text-id="8492579284278796922" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_960965308" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/960965308" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/960965308?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=cotton-candy">cotton-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer960965308" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer921647046925728484">Buddy Read with my KA loving friends at at <a>Buddies Books & Baubles</a><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“Layne knew he was in love with her. Not only that, he’d never stopped loving her. Not once, not for a second, not for twenty-one years.</i>
</blockquote><br/>A few of my favorite tropes in my cotton candy reading are….Lovers separated for years and then brought back together and a fake marriage that turns into love ♥♥♥ I’m a sucker for both of those. So Golden Trail didn’t even have to work very hard for me to like it because it has long lost lover</span>
  <span id="freeText921647046925728484" style="display:none">Buddy Read with my KA loving friends at at <a>Buddies Books &amp; Baubles</a><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Layne knew he was in love with her. Not only that, he’d never stopped loving her. Not once, not for a second, not for twenty-one years.</i>
</blockquote><br />A few of my favorite tropes in my cotton candy reading are….Lovers separated for years and then brought back together and a fake marriage that turns into love ♥♥♥ I’m a sucker for both of those. So Golden Trail didn’t even have to work very hard for me to like it because it has long lost lovers reunited and while they don’t get married they do fake a relationship until they don’t.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“It’s not fake is it?” Jasper asked softly and Layne studied his son thinking he had vastly underestimated Jasper too. <br />“It was, Jas, it isn’t anymore.” Jasper nodded. Layne continued. “She doesn’t know that yet, though.”<br />Jasper stared at him then his mouth twitched before, very slowly, it spread into a smile.” </i>
</blockquote><br />Okay so Tanner and Rocky aren’t perfect. I liked Tanner Layne for the most part. He is a good dad and part of the Alpha boys club. While I thought at times he was a huge jerk (This is just something KA does and I’ve accepted it) mostly to his ex-wife and in the beginning to Rocky overall he seems like a pretty good guy.<br /><br />Rocky I totally liked though. She is tough and fights to be different in a world full of conformity. As an English teacher at the local high school she is excited about teaching and doing it in a way that engages the kids she has in her classes. I loved that about her.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“See, that's the beauty of books. We get to take what we want out of them and it can be different for everyone. You get a good one, you may even find what you need.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I really enjoyed the wooing the Tanner throws down to win her back into his life. I also couldn’t wait to find out how things went so wrong in the past that they had to spend all that time apart. I was not what I thought it was and I appreciate the originality of it.<br /><br />KA went a little darker in this than I expected and the bad guys that they are looking for are BAD. I loved how the kids got to have a slice of the action in this and how they played their part in the story. What was happening in that town was really heartbreaking when we find out how bad it was. <br /><br />But there are also the fun moments to battle the emotional ones and as always KA is a great storyteller. She needs to sometimes tone down the details of the clothing, throw pillows and side characters but sometimes that seems like the charm of her stories too. That and all the cameos from people we love in the other books. It is great to see Colt Feb and the baby. I loved seeing Joe with Kerra as she starts dating *snickers*. And KA always has a great cast of side characters and this is no exception. If KA is your cup of tea then this books should hit all the high points.<br /><br /><b>Warning</b>: <i>Layne can be and alpha ass at times. I expect this in a KA book and just let it go. He isn't a KA alpha badass until he backs the heroine against the wall so they can 'talk'. If that isn't your thing then you will probably hate most of the book. </i><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="921647046925728484" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_247542031" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/247542031" />
    <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz"><img alt="Elizabeth (Liz)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551206872p2/5495317.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/247542031?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elizabeth (Liz)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elizabeth (Liz)" href="/user/show/5495317-elizabeth-liz">Elizabeth (Liz)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=5-star-reads">5-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=ebook-read">ebook-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5495317-elizabeth-liz?shelf=romantic-suspense-read">romantic-suspense-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer247542031" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7363110202502510452">5 stars<br/><br/>Still not sure about her parenting techniques (like, not AT ALL), but, again, KA managed to drag me into a fascinating story and keep me riveted to the very end. Rocky's breakdown, toward the end, is very hard to read, and, if you have any triggers for panic/PTSD/etc, be aware that scene might possibly set you off. It was a little too real, in my opinion. <br/><br/>Quite a story. I don't know how she keeps doing this.<br/><br/>*Revised to 5 stars 2/29/12 as I find myself continually thinking about this book,</span>
  <span id="freeText7363110202502510452" style="display:none">5 stars<br /><br />Still not sure about her parenting techniques (like, not AT ALL), but, again, KA managed to drag me into a fascinating story and keep me riveted to the very end. Rocky's breakdown, toward the end, is very hard to read, and, if you have any triggers for panic/PTSD/etc, be aware that scene might possibly set you off. It was a little too real, in my opinion. <br /><br />Quite a story. I don't know how she keeps doing this.<br /><br />*Revised to 5 stars 2/29/12 as I find myself continually thinking about this book, particularly the long scene of Rocky teaching To Kill A Mockingbird to her highschool class, as well as the scene where she has a breakdown. Kristen writes in such a way that you truly, actually, feel you're right there. So much emotion. Love it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="7363110202502510452" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_712770197" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/712770197" />
    <a title="TeriLyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1459307-terilyn"><img alt="TeriLyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396453806p2/1459307.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/712770197?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TeriLyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TeriLyn" href="/user/show/1459307-terilyn">TeriLyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1459307-terilyn?shelf=2014-favorites">2014-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1459307-terilyn?shelf=re-reads">re-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1459307-terilyn?shelf=2013-favorites">2013-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer712770197" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9068958241094250054"><br/><b> 5 <i>Golden Trail</i> Stars</b><br/><br/>It feels like I’ve said this at least one thousand times: Kristen Ashley takes the ordinary and makes it extraordinary. Seriously, I can't get enough. Every single time I sit down with on her books it’s like magic dancing off the pages and into my mind. The ‘Burg series, each a contemporary romance, delivers the usual KA bad ass alphas, the kick ass heroines and non-stop action. This read marks the second time I’ve read <i>Golden Trail</i> and it was even more phenomenal than the f</span>
  <span id="freeText9068958241094250054" style="display:none"><br /><b> 5 <i>Golden Trail</i> Stars</b><br /><br />It feels like I’ve said this at least one thousand times: Kristen Ashley takes the ordinary and makes it extraordinary. Seriously, I can't get enough. Every single time I sit down with on her books it’s like magic dancing off the pages and into my mind. The ‘Burg series, each a contemporary romance, delivers the usual KA bad ass alphas, the kick ass heroines and non-stop action. This read marks the second time I’ve read <i>Golden Trail</i> and it was even more phenomenal than the first time. Kristen Ashley will always get you out of book rut if you’re in one and she’ll always entertain you for hours on end with engaging characters, witty dialogue, and excellently written tales of life and love. This author proves herself time and again with readers when without fail you fall in love with characters, even if they anger you, because she stays true to those characters and the stories she believes making a believer out of you too. It’s comedy, it’s mystery, it’s action-adventure all rolled into a great romance. <br /> <br /><i>Golden Trail</i> gives us the amazing Tanner Layne – bad ass extraordinaire, hot private investigator; he's bossy yet patient, he's brutally honest yet incredibly kind. Layne loves so fiercely your heart skips a beat every time he turns on the sweet. He’s a strong alpha, a strong man who makes no excuses for his actions and defends any convictions he believes. He's a man who likes a challenge even in his women. Once scorned by the love of his life, Raquel Merrick, Layne lets his attitude fly at the beginning but stick it out with him because you will not be disappointed in the ride. Layne’s love for Rocky never wavered even after years of separation. Raquel Merrick proves to be a 'warrior'; she's soft, she's kind, she's loyal, she's fiercely protective, she puts a smile on her face so no one will see her demons and she, too, makes no excuses for what she believes and defends those convictions. Her strength comes from the belief in Layne and his protection. She grows stronger throughout the book. And she wears big T-shirts to bed – yes, that’s cool to me. <br /><br /><i>Golden Trail</i> differs from other books in this series in that the story is told strictly from Layne’s point of view. It’s an interesting choice to live this story fully through Layne’s eyes whereas in other books the POV switches between hero and heroine. Layne’s views of the world seep into your heart making you fall in love with him that much more. It was also a smart choice because I’m not sure how Rocky would come across with what’s constantly going on in her head. Through Layne we see and believe in the powerful love him and Rocky share; a love that withstood the test of time even after major betrayal and heartbreak so many years ago. <br /> <br />I would be remiss not to mention the secondary cast present in this book as they add so many extra layers of emotion and depth to the story. Specifically, Layne's beyond awesome teenage boys. The relationship between the boys and Layne led to hilarious interactions and incredible growth. Jasper, Layne’s oldest, procures a relationship with Joe Callahan’s step daughter Kiera resulting in extra funny moments and another beautiful love story. Vera (Layne’s mother) &amp; Devin (his mentor) add more great comedy. My favorite of these secondary characters is the introduction of Ryker, Layne’s kinda/sorta investigating partner. There are some seriously funny moments with Ryker that will have you laughing out loud and also moments where this big, scary man leads to you tears. He and Layne form a great bond. You get more Joe Callahan which, let’s face it, who doesn’t love that? Violet too, along with Colt and Feb and the rest of The ‘Burg crew.<br /><br />Overall, <i>Golden Trail</i> gives you exactly what you want from a Kristen Ashley novel but this time through the sole point of view of the hero. Layne and Rocky’s romance proves to be unconventional, at times very sad and heart breaking yet through it all Ms. Ashley reminds of strength, faith in love, and the importance of solid family – no matter what kind of family. Finally, Kristen Ashley provides us with one her <b>EPIC</b> epilogues. These epilogues remind why I read romance. <b>Pure KA magic</b>. And seriously? Tanner Layne working his own bad-ass-magic to get the bad guys? You just can’t miss this. <br /><br /><b>Favorite Quotes:</b><br /><br /><i>“…Layne knew he was in love with her. Not only that, he’d never stopped loving her. Not once, not for a second, not for twenty-one years.”<br /><br />“You’re cute as hell when you get pissed. You always were cute as hell when you got pissed. I used to piss you off just to see you get pissed, I liked it so much.”<br /><br />“You know, one of the reasons I fell in love with you was because you were always honest. With everyone, including me. I loved that. It made me feel safe. I still love that about you, especially knowing it takes courage to be honest. Your courage, I love that about you too.”</i><br /><br /><br /><br />First Read - October 2013<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9068958241094250054" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
